                        </span>

normal'>your</b> principal to the obligations on the part of a <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> and to enter into a <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>contract</b> for the purchase of a <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>lot</b> on behalf of <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>your</b> principal on the terms of a <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

                    <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";

            <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;line-height:150%'>
                <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    An amendment or addition to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>conditions</b> or to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>particulars</b> or to both whether
                    contained in a supplement to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>catalogue</b>,
                    a written notice from the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>auctioneers</b>

                    </span>

            <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;line-height:150%'>
                <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    Subject to <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>condition G</b>9(3):<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

            <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;line-height:150%'>
                <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    (a) the date specified in the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>special conditions</b>; or<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

            <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;line-height:150%'>
                <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    (b) if no date is specified, 20 <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>business days</b> after the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>contract date</b>;<o:p></o:p>
                </span>

                    Unless the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> and the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>buyer</b> otherwise agree, completion cannot take place until both have
                    complied with their obligations under the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>contract</b>
                    and the balance of the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>price</b> is
                    unconditionally received in the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>’s
                    conveyancer’s client account.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

                    other than the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>’s default the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> must pay interest at the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>interest rate</b> on the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>price</b> (less any deposit paid) from the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>agreed completion date</b> up to and
                    including the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>actual completion date</b>.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-17.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l13 level3 lfo20;
tab-stops:list 68.05pt'>
                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:
"Calibri","sans-serif";mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>
                        i.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> must comply with the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b>’s reasonable requirements unless
                    to do so would (but for the indemnity in paragraph (iii)) expose the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> to a liability that the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> would not otherwise have, in
                    which case the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> may act
                    reasonably in such a way as to avoid that liability;<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

            <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:68.05pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-17.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l13 level3 lfo20;
tab-stops:list 68.05pt'>
                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:

mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>
                        ii.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    if the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> gives the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>buyer</b> notice of the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>’s
                    intended act and the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> does not
                    object within five <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>business days</b>
                    giving reasons for the objection the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>
                    may act as the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> intends; and<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

            <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:68.05pt;mso-add-space:

tab-stops:list 68.05pt'>
                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:

mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>
                        iii.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> is to indemnify the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> against all loss or liability
                    the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> incurs through acting as
                    the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> requires, or by reason of
                    delay caused by the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b>.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

                    to money by way of rent deposit in respect of a <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

                    and 7 of that Act and that the requisite majority of qualifying tenants has not
                    accepted the offer.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

                <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";

            </p>

                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>
                        G19.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><u>
                    <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                        Sale by <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>practitioner</b><o:p></o:p>
                    </span>
                </u>

                    This <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>condition</b> G19 applies where the sale is
                    by a <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>practitioner</b> either as <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> or as agent of the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>.<o:p></o:p>

                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:

                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>

                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    The <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> must notify the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> of those employees whose
                    contracts of employment will transfer to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>buyer</b> on <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>completion</b> (the
                    “Transferring Employees”).<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>This
                    notification must be given to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b>
                    not less than 14 days before <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>completion</b>.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>

                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    payments on
                    account (whether received or still then due from a tenant) exceed attributable
                    service charge expenditure, the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>
                    must pay to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> an amount
                    equal to the excess when it provides the service charge account;<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

            <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:68.05pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-17.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l13 level3 lfo20;
tab-stops:list 68.05pt'>
                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:
"Calibri","sans-serif";mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>
                        ii.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    attributable
                    service charge expenditure exceeds payments on account (whether those payments
                    have been received or are still then due), the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>buyer</b> must use all reasonable endeavours to recover the shortfall
                    from the tenant at the next service charge reconciliation date and pay the
                    amount so recovered to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>
                    within five <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>business days</b> of receipt
                    in cleared funds;<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

            <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:51.05pt;text-align:justify;line-height:
150%'>
                <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    but in respect of payments on
                    account that are still due from a tenant <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>condition</b>
                    G11 (<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>arrears</b>) applies. <o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";

                    In respect
                    of service charge expenditure that is not attributable to any <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>tenancy</b> the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>seller</b> must pay the expenditure incurred in respect of the period
                    before <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>actual completion date</b> and
                    the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> must pay the expenditure
                    incurred in respect of the period after <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>
                        actual
                        completion date
                    </b>. Any necessary monetary adjustment is to be made within
                    five <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>business days</b> of the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> providing the service charge
                    account to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b>.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>

                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:

                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    If a rent
                    review is agreed or determined before <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>completion</b>
                    but the increased rent and any interest recoverable from the tenant has not
                    been received by <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>completion</b> the
                    increased rent and any interest recoverable is to be treated as <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>arrears</b>.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

                <span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";

                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>
                        (8)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";

                    The <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> and the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

                    negotiations and proceedings.<o:p></o:p>

                    under a <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>tenancy</b> has the right to
                    remain in occupation under part II of the Landlord and Tenant Act 1954 (as

                    with the
                    co-operation of the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> take
                    immediate steps to substitute itself as a party to any proceedings;<o:p></o:p>

                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:

                        </span>
                    </span>

                    use all
                    reasonable endeavours to conclude any proceedings or negotiations for the
                    renewal of the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>tenancy</b> and the

                    of ownership of the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>lot</b> within five <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>business days</b> of receipt of cleared
                    funds.<o:p></o:p>

                    warranty is assignable the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b>
                    must:<o:p></o:p>

            <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:68.05pt;mso-add-space:

                    on <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>completion</b> assign it to the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> and give notice of assignment to
                    the person who gave the warranty; and<o:p></o:p>
                </span>

            <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:68.05pt;mso-add-space:

                <![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:

mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    <span style='mso-list:Ignore'>
                        ii.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
                            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
                        </span>
                    </span>
                </span><![endif]><span lang=EN-GB style='font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>
                    apply for
                    (and the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>seller</b> and the <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>buyer</b> must use all reasonable
                    endeavours to obtain) any consent to assign that is required. If consent has
                    not been obtained by <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>completion</b> the
                    warranty must be assigned within five <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>
                        business
                        days
                    </b> after the consent has been obtained.<o:p></o:p>
                </span>
            </p>

            <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;line-height:150%'>
